***протыкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:протыкать.html>протыка́ть</a> (30911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протыкать.html>протыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">protykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проткнуть.html>проткну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pierce <i>(through)</i>, to transfix, to pink, to spit, to skewer</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протыкать.html>проты́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">protýkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:протыкать.html>протыка́ть</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make many (holes) in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pierce in several places</li></ol>

***протягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивать</a> (3676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">протяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">protjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">protjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch, to extend</li>
<li>to hold / stretch / reach out; to extend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>protjágivatʹ</b> rúku pómošči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to extend a helping hand to smb.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to delay, to drag out</li>
<li>to drawl, to prolong, to sustain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдать.html>вы́дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кредит.html>креди́т</a>,</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne mogú výdatʹ vam étot kredít,</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:обреченно.html>обречённо</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>.</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="None mention e-example" lang="ru">I cannot give you this credit</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I cannot give you this credit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he drawled resignedly.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold out, to live a while longer, to last <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">survive</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протя́нет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On dólgo ne <b>protjánet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">He won't last (live) long.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>protjágivatʹ</b> nógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn up one's toes; to kick the bucket</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***протяженность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:протяженность.html>протяжённость</a> (18264)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протяженный.html>протяжённый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">protjažónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протяженность.html>протяжённость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">protjažónnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протяженность.html>протяжённости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протяженность.html>протяжённости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протяженность.html>протяжённостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>extent, length</li></ol>

***протянуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́ть</a> (831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">protjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch, to extend</li>
<li>to hold / stretch / reach out; to extend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>protjanútʹ</b> rúku pómošči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to extend a helping hand to smb.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to delay, to drag out</li>
<li>to drawl, to prolong, to sustain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдать.html>вы́дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кредит.html>креди́т</a>,</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne mogú výdatʹ vam étot kredít,</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:обреченно.html>обречённо</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>.</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="None mention e-example" lang="ru">I cannot give you this credit</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I cannot give you this credit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he drawled resignedly.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold out, to live a while longer, to last <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">survive</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протя́нет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On dólgo ne <b>protjánet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">He won't last (live) long.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>protjanútʹ</b> nógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn up one's toes; to kick the bucket</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуться.html>протяну́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">protjanútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуть.html>протяну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">protjanútʹ nógi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проучить.html>проучи́ть</a> (17138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проучить.html>проучи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proučítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проу́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to teach <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for some time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to teach (someone) a lesson</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">profanus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unholy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:профан.html>профа́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">profán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:профан.html>профа́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:профан.html>профа́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:профан.html>профа́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ignoramus (totally ignorant person)</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проха́живать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proxáživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прохвост.html>прохво́ст</a> (16957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">профос</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">profos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, finally from German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Profoss</i> (cognate of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">provost</i>)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прохвост.html>прохво́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proxvóst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прохвост.html>прохво́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прохвост.html>прохво́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прохвост.html>прохво́стов</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scoundrel, rascal, fraud</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прохладный.html>прохла́дный</a> (4498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хла́дный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xládnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прохладный.html>прохла́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proxládnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прохла́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прохла́дней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прохла́днейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cool (<i>temperature</i>)</li></ol>
